## Analysis: dotazy / dev-env

### 1. Identity

**Project:** `dev-env` вҖ” a portable developer environment bootstrap system  
**Owner:** `doma77git` (GitHub: `doma77git/dev-env`)  
**Version:** `v1.1.1` (released today, 2026-05-31)  
**License:** MIT  
**Local path:** `C:\Projects\dotazy` (local clone name differs from upstream)  
**Summary:** One-command developer environment provisioning for Windows (PS7) and Linux/WSL. Detects machine вҶ’ fingerprints вҶ’ profiles вҶ’ installs вҶ’ repairs вҶ’ validates.

---

### 2. Architecture & Pipeline

Four layers, strict dependency direction:

```
GIST (3 entry files)        вҶҗ bootstrap entry point, minimal surface
  вҶ“
REPO (this workspace)       вҶҗ all scripts, configs, profiles, docs
  вҶ“
LOCAL (~/.dev-env/)         вҶҗ machine state: reports, clone, logs, config
  вҶ“
PAGES (GitHub Pages)        вҶҗ docs/dev-env/index.md вҶ’ landing page
```

Pipeline runs in numbered phase order. Each script is self-contained. No framework, no module вҖ” straight PowerShell with conventions:

| Phase | Script | Role | Mutates? |
|-------|--------|------|----------|
| 00 | `00-core-check.ps1` | Prerequisites: PS7, git, connectivity | No |
| 30 | `30-clone.ps1` | Clone/pull repo to `~/.dev-env/repo/` | Git only |
| 10 | `10-detect.ps1` | Fingerprint + 18-tool inventory | No |
| 20 | `20-report.ps1` / `20-install-software.ps1` | Display + save JSON / winget install | Yes (install) |
| 40 | `40-profile.ps1` | Detect home/work/lab/server + git identity | Writes config |
| 50 | `50-setup-{home,lab,work,server}.ps1` | Profile-specific setup | Yes (ShouldProcess) |
| 60 | `60-repair.ps1` | PATH dedup, HOME, OneDrive, SSH | Yes (ShouldProcess) |
| 70 | `70-test.ps1` | 17 validation checks | No |
| 90 | `90-wt-profile.ps1` | Windows Terminal DevEnv profile | Yes |
| 95 | `95-dashboard.ps1` | HTML dashboard from reports | No |
| 99 | `99-validate-bootstrap.ps1` | End-to-end pipeline validation | No |

---

### 3. Profile System (Key Design Choice)

JSON profile hierarchy, class-based inheritance:

```
profiles/base.json           вҶҗ shared defaults (required tools, git config, secrets list)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ profiles/home.json     вҶҗ unrestricted personal machine
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ profiles/work.json     вҶҗ corporate: proxy, safeMode
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ profiles/lab.json      вҶҗ experimental: WSL, scoop
  в””в”Җв”Җ profiles/server.json   вҶҗ headless: safeMode, no GUI
```

`extends` field controls inheritance. Profile auto-detection runs in `40-profile.ps1` вҖ” domain lookup вҶ’ OS caption вҶ’ manufacturer вҶ’ proxy check вҶ’ fallback to home.

Ship shape. The schema for detection reports lives in `ai/schema.json` вҖ” JSON Schema draft 2020-12, covering `meta`, `status`, `fingerprint`, `os`, `tools`, `features`, and `pipeline` results.

---

### 4. Safety Model

This is the project's strongest characteristic. Every destructive operation is guarded:

- **`SupportsShouldProcess`** вҖ” every setup/repair/configure script supports `-WhatIf` and `-Confirm`
- **`safeMode`** вҖ” work and server profiles enforce dry-run-first; no automatic installs
- **`Confirm-Action.ps1`** вҖ” interactive 10s timeout prompt; headless environments auto-skip
- **`Start-Transcript`** вҖ” phases 50-60 log to `~/.dev-env/logs/`
- **`undo-last.ps1`** вҖ” parses last transcript and gives rollback guidance
- **`machines.json`** вҖ” append-only, never committed, never synced

CI runs `continue-on-error: true` on known-ephemeral checks (OneDrive, SSH), which is the correct call for a bootstrap that can't control the runner environment.

---

### 5. CI/CD & Quality

Five workflows in `.github/workflows/`:

- **`ci.yml`** вҖ” push to master/main: Windows (00 вҶ’ 70) + Linux (bash dry-run) + context.md sync check
- **`pr.yml`** вҖ” PR validation
- **`full-test.yml`** вҖ” likely matrix test across Windows Server 2022/2025 and PS7.2/7.4
- **`gist-sync.yml`** вҖ” syncs bootstrap files to GitHub Gist
- **`validate-agents.yml`** вҖ” ensures AGENTS.md and related AI files stay current

---

### 6. Git State & Surface Issues

```
Branch: master (ahead of origin/master)
```

*Modified tracked files:*
- `.gitignore` вҖ” local additions (not pushed)
- `AGENTS.md` вҖ” project instructions populated by CodeWhale
- `manifest.json` вҖ” updated locally

*Untracked files:*
- `REASONIX.md` вҖ” Reasonix agent rules
- `apply-all.ps1`, `apply-updates.ps1`, `sync-all.ps1`, `sync-all-packed.ps1`, `sync-updates.ps1` вҖ” sync utility scripts (look like local helpers)
- `onedrive-vylepseni.patch`, `patches.txt`, `patch_out.txt` вҖ” scratch/patch files

**Notable:** The repo folder is named `dotazy` locally but the upstream is `dev-env`. The `.gitignore` has local additions. Several patch/scratch files are untracked and should probably be excluded from accidental commits.

---

### 7. Pending Work (from manifest.json and git log)

From `ai/context.md` todo list:

| Item | Status |
|------|--------|
| InteraktivnГӯ reЕҫim v `setup-*.ps1` вҖ” vГҪbДӣr packages, identity prompt | **Pending** |
| SSH keygen prompt v setupu вҖ” kdyЕҫ chybГӯ klГӯДҚe, nabГӯdnout `ssh-keygen` | **Pending** |

Both are UX improvements to the setup scripts вҖ” adding interactive package selection and fallback SSH key generation during profile-specific setup.

---

### Summary

Cohesive, well-architested PowerShell bootstrap with a strong safety contract. The profile inheritance model, WhatIf-first convention, and CI matrix give it the structure of a production tool rather than a personal dotfiles repo. Two small UX items remain open. The local clone has some drift from upstream (untracked helpers, patched manifest) that should be reconciled before a push.

## Complete Analysis: dev-env (dotazy)

---

### 1. Project Identity

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| **Name** | `dev-env` |
| **Local clone** | `C:\Projects\dotazy` |
| **Owner** | `doma77git` |
| **Version** | `v1.1.1` (released 2026-05-31) |
| **License** | MIT |
| **Primary language** | PowerShell 7+ (Windows) + Bash 4+ (Linux/WSL) |
| **CI** | GitHub Actions вҖ” 5 workflows |
| **Entry points** | `bootstrap.ps1` (Win), `bootstrap.sh` (Linux), `00-bootstrap-fallback.ps1` (PS5) |

---

### 2. Architecture

**Four layers, strict dependency direction:**

```
GIST (3 entry files)      вҶҗ bootstrap.ps1, bootstrap.sh, 00-bootstrap-fallback.ps1
  вҶ“
REPO (this workspace)     вҶҗ all scripts, configs, profiles, docs, AI context
  вҶ“
LOCAL (~/.dev-env/)       вҶҗ machines.json, reports, clone, config, logs
  вҶ“
PAGES (GitHub Pages)      вҶҗ docs/index.md вҶ’ doma77git.github.io/dev-env
```

**Pipeline phases (numbered, each self-contained):**

```
bootstrap.ps1 / bootstrap.sh
  в”ңв”Җ 00  CORE CHECK     вҖ” PS7, git, connectivity (never installs)
  в”ңв”Җ 30  CLONE           вҖ” git clone/pull ~/.dev-env/repo/ (always runs, read-only)
  в”ңв”Җ 10  DETECT          вҖ” fingerprint, OS, 18 tools, PATH, OneDrive, corporate signals
  в”ңв”Җ 20  REPORT          вҖ” JSON display + save to ~/.dev-env/ + machines.json
  в”Ӯ      INSTALL          вҖ” winget package installation by category (ShouldProcess)
  в”ңв”Җ 40  PROFILE         вҖ” auto-detect home/work/lab/server + git identity + SSH + GPG
  в”ңв”Җ 50  SETUP           вҖ” per-profile setup dispatcher (ShouldProcess, transcript)
  в”ңв”Җ 60  REPAIR          вҖ” PATH dedup, HOME, OneDrive, SSH (ShouldProcess, backup)
  в”ңв”Җ 70  TEST            вҖ” 16 validation checks вҶ’ exit 0/1
  в”ңв”Җ 90  WT PROFILE      вҖ” Windows Terminal DevEnv profile
  в”ңв”Җ 95  DASHBOARD       вҖ” HTML dashboard from logs
  в””в”Җ 99  VALIDATE        вҖ” end-to-end pipeline validation
```

**Key design decision:** Phase 00, 10, 30 are read-only. Phases 20 (install), 50, 60 have `SupportsShouldProcess` + `-WhatIf` + `-Confirm`. All destructive operations log transcripts.

---

### 3. Profile System

JSON inheritance via `extends` field. Auto-detection in `40-profile.ps1`:

```
profiles/base.json           вҶҗ shared: required tools, git config, secrets, sync rules
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ profiles/home.json     вҶҗ personal PC, unrestricted
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ profiles/work.json     вҶҗ corporate: proxy, safeMode, GPG signing
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ profiles/lab.json      вҶҗ VM: WSL, scoop, experimental
  в””в”Җв”Җ profiles/server.json   вҶҗ headless: safeMode, no GUI, minimal toolchain
```

Detection priority: saved profile > domain-joined > server OS > WSL > proxy > VM > domain DNS > home fallback. The `40-profile.ps1` also runs `Merge-Deep` for recursive profile merging and validates JSON structure.

---

### 4. Safety Model (Strongest Feature)

| Mechanism | Scope | Details |
|-----------|-------|---------|
| **WhatIf** | All setup/repair/configure | PowerShell `SupportsShouldProcess` + Bash `$DRY_RUN` |
| **safeMode** | work/server profiles | Blocks auto-install entirely; requires `-Force` to override |
| **Confirm-Action** | Interactive phases | 10s timeout, headless detection вҶ’ auto-skip |
| **Transcript** | Phases 50-60 | `Start-Transcript` вҶ’ `~/.dev-env/logs/` |
| **Backup** | Phase 60 | Pre-repair backup вҶ’ `~/.dev-env/backups/<timestamp>/` |
| **undo-last.ps1** | Post-hoc | Parses last transcript and gives rollback guidance |
| **machines.json** | Every run | Append-only, never committed, never synced |
| **Secrets inventory** | `base.json#/secrets` | Canonical list of what must never be committed |

---

### 5. CI/CD Pipeline вҖ” 5 Workflows

| Workflow | Trigger | What it does |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| **ci.yml** | Push to master | Windows (00вҶ’70) + Linux (bash dry-run) + context.md sync check |
| **pr.yml** | PR to master | Windows + Linux + context sync check |
| **full-test.yml** | Schedule (weekly) + manual | Matrix: win2022+win2025 Г— PS7.2+PS7.4; full pipeline run |
| **gist-sync.yml** | Release published | Auto-syncs `bootstrap.ps1`, `bootstrap.sh`, `00-bootstrap-fallback.ps1` to Gist |
| **validate-agents.yml** | Push/PR on AGENTS.md or scripts | PSScriptAnalyzer linting + AGENTS.md phase table vs actual scripts + header validation |

**Quality tooling also includes:**
- `.github/agents/docs-verify.agent.md` вҖ” documentation accuracy agent with 6-point checklist
- `.github/agents/ps-review.agent.md` вҖ” PowerShell code review agent with 17-point checklist
- `.github/hooks/format-ps1.json` + `auto-format-ps1.ps1` + `check-ps1-format.ps1` вҖ” formatting hooks
- `.github/instructions/powershell.instructions.md` вҖ” detailed PowerShell conventions
- `.github/prompts/new-phase.prompt.md` вҖ” prompts for adding new pipeline phases

---

### 6. Linux/WSL Parity (bootstrap.sh)

`bootstrap.sh` at 490 lines is a full port of the Windows pipeline for Linux. Key observations:

- **Covers phases 00вҶ’30вҶ’10вҶ’20вҶ’40вҶ’50** (no 60/70 in shell вҖ” repair and test rely on PowerShell)
- **Self-contained inline JSON generation** вҖ” no `jq` dependency
- **`machines.json` append logic** вҖ” manual JSON array manipulation via `head`/`tail`/`mv`
- **Multi-package manager support** вҖ” `apt`, `brew`, `dnf`, `pacman`, `apk`
- **WSL detection** via `/proc/version` grepping for `microsoft`
- **Profile detection** mirrors PowerShell: server OS вҶ’ WSL вҶ’ proxy вҶ’ VM вҶ’ domain DNS вҶ’ home
- **`$DEV_ENV_WHATIF`** as environment variable for dry-run (Bash's WhatIf equivalent)
- **Node/Python install coverage** across all 5 package managers

**Gap vs Windows:** No 60-repair or 70-test in bash; no transcript logging; no backup mechanism.

---

### 7. Key Script Sizes & Complexity

| Script | Lines | Role |
|--------|-------|------|
| `bootstrap.ps1` | 105 | Windows entry orchestrator |
| `bootstrap.sh` | 490 | Linux/WSL entry (self-contained) |
| `scripts/10-detect.ps1` | 607 | Full environment inventory engine |
| `scripts/60-repair.ps1` | 605 | PATH, OneDrive, SSH, HOME repair |
| `scripts/20-install-software.ps1` | 190 | winget package installation |
| `scripts/40-profile.ps1` | 242 | Profile auto-detection + merge |
| `scripts/70-test.ps1` | ~170 | 16 validation checks |
| `ai/context.md` | 461 | Full AI context |

### 8. Git State & Local Drift

```
Branch: master (ahead of origin/master)
```

**Modified tracked files:**
- `.gitignore` вҖ” local additions
- `AGENTS.md` вҖ” populated by CodeWhale with template scaffolding
- `manifest.json` вҖ” `updated` date bumped locally

**Untracked files (all local helpers/patch files):**
- `REASONIX.md` вҖ” Reasonix working knowledge (71 lines of project reference)
- `sync-all.ps1`, `sync-all-packed.ps1`, `apply-all.ps1`, `apply-updates.ps1`, `sync-updates.ps1`
- `onedrive-vylepseni.patch`, `patches.txt`, `patch_out.txt`

**Recommendation:** `onedrive-vylepseni.patch`, `patches.txt`, `patch_out.txt` should be added to `.gitignore` вҖ” they're ephemeral scratch files. The sync scripts may warrant keeping, possibly in a `tools/` directory.

---

### 9. Pending Work (from manifest.json + ai/context.md)

| Item | Priority | Details |
|------|----------|---------|
| **Interactive mode in setup-*.ps1** | Medium | Package selection prompts, identity configuration during setup phase |
| **SSH keygen prompt in setup** | Low | Offer `ssh-keygen -t ed25519` when no keys found |

Both are UX enhancements to the setup phase вҖ” neither is a blocker.

---

### 10. Test Coverage (scripts/70-test.ps1)

The test script validates 16 checks:

1. OS is Windows 10/11
2. HOME is set
3. `~/.dev-env/` directory exists
4. Git installed + `user.name` + `user.email`
5. Node.js installed
6. Python installed
7. VS Code installed
8. PATH entries < 50
9. PATH no duplicates (system/user/cross-scope detection)
10. `~/.ssh/` exists
11. SSH key exists
12. Profile JSONs valid (extends + identity checks)
13. Required packages installed
14. Reasonix installed
15. OneDrive not redirecting system folders (Desktop, Documents, Pictures, Music, Videos)
16. Exit code 0/1 with pass/fail summary

**Test output includes actionable fix suggestions per failing check** вҖ” e.g. `"Fix: winget install Git.Git"` вҖ” which is valuable for headless/CI runs.

---

### 11. Anomalies & Observations

1. **Repo name mismatch**: Local directory is `dotazy`, upstream is `dev-env`. Not a problem for local work but could confuse `git remote` references.

2. **AGENTS.md is a template shell**: All sections are commented-out HTML comments вҖ” no actual project guidance filled in. The `validate-agents.yml` CI workflow tries to extract a phase table from it, but the file currently has none.

3. **`70-test.ps1` claims "16 checks"** in its header but the badge in README says "17 tests". The test loop is 16 explicit checks. This is a doc mismatch.

4. **`60-repair.ps1`** has a `-SkipBackup` param with `"(testing only)"` description вҖ” this is the correct pattern for CI but worth documenting more prominently.

5. **`bootstrap.sh` machines.json handling**: Uses `head -n -1` to strip trailing `]` then appends вҖ” fragile if the file is empty or has exactly one entry (edge case on first run where file was just created with `[` + json + `]`). Actually on first run lines 229-233 handle it: `echo "[" > file; cat report >> file; echo "]" >> file`. On subsequent runs, head strips the last line (the `]`), appends a comma + new entry + new `]`. This works but is fragile if the file gets malformed.

6. **Gist sync workflow** uses `secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN` вҖ” but `gh gist edit` requires a token with `gist` scope. `GITHUB_TOKEN` in a release workflow **does** have `contents: write` but may not have `gist` scope. This likely fails silently or needs a PAT secret added.

7. **The `index.html`** at root is a local offline landing page вҖ” not referenced from any CI workflow or documented route. Its purpose could be clearer.

---

### 12. Recommendations

| # | Area | Suggestion |
|---|------|------------|
| 1 | **Git hygiene** | Add `*.patch`, `patch_out.txt`, `patches.txt` to `.gitignore` |
| 2 | **AGENTS.md** | Populate with actual project information (or remove the validate-agents.yml check that requires it) |
| 3 | **Doc mismatch** | Fix `70-test.ps1` header: "16 checks" вҶ’ update README badge from 17 to 16, or add the 17th check |
| 4 | **Gist sync** | Verify `GITHUB_TOKEN` has gist scope, or switch to `secrets.GH_PAT` with explicit scope |
| 5 | **Linux parity** | Consider a `/bin/dev-env-check` script for Linux that replicates the 70-test checks in bash |
| 6 | **Pending UX** | The interactive mode and SSH keygen prompt are small wins that would improve first-run experience |
| 7 | **Phase numbering** | Phases jump from 00 to 30 to 10 to 20 вҖ” this is by design (read-only first, then report, then mutate) but worth an explicit comment somewhere for new contributors |

---

**Conclusion:** This is a production-quality bootstrap system. The safety model is the standout design decision вҖ” every destructive path is guarded, logged, and reversible. The Linux port is thorough. Two small UX items and a handful of doc mismatches remain. The local clone has some drift from upstream that should be reconciled before a push.

---

### рҹ”ҙ Critical Issue: AGENTS.md is Empty

`AGENTS.md` is the entry point for all AI tools (Copilot, Claude Code, Cursor, Codex). It contains only HTML comment placeholders:

```html
<!-- Add build/test commands here -->
<!-- Describe the high-level structure... -->
<!-- How should an AI agent approach this project? -->
```

Every section вҖ” architecture, entry points, key modules, data flow, cache stability вҖ” is blank. The `validate-agents.yml` CI workflow tries to parse a phase table from it (which doesn't exist) and would fail if run against the current file. The `copilot-instructions.md` at root tells agents to "Start with `AGENTS.md`" for the decision tree вҖ” but there's nothing there.

---

### рҹҹЎ Inconsistency: Test Count Drift

The number of validation checks varies across **7 documents**:

| Source | Claims | Actual |
|--------|--------|--------|
| `scripts/70-test.ps1` header | "16 checks" | **17** individual `check()` calls (with git installed) |
| `README.md` badge | "17 checks" | вң… matches maximum |
| `README.md` phase table | "16 kontrol" | вҡ пёҸ off by 1 |
| `docs/index.md` phase table | "17 kontrol" | вң… matches maximum |
| `docs/index.md` scripts table | "15 kontrol" | вҡ пёҸ off by 2 |
| `docs/architecture.md` (line 73) | "15 checks" | вҡ пёҸ off by 2 |
| `ai/context.md` (line 52-53) | "14 checks" | вҡ пёҸ off by 3 |
| `copilot-instructions.md` | "17 validation checks" | вң… matches maximum |

**Root cause:** Git user.name and user.email are conditional (only run when git is found). On a machine with git: 17 checks. Without git: 15. The header says 16, which is wrong for both cases.

---

### рҹҹЎ Stale Version / Date

`docs/index.md` footer says `*dev-env v1.1.0 В· 2026-05-30*`. `manifest.json` says `"version": "1.1.1"`, `"updated": "2026-05-31"`. The landing page doc is one version and one day behind.

This is visible in the rendered output and affects the tree hierarchy.

**Assistant:**

## `scripts/99-validate-bootstrap.ps1` вҖ” Review

The file is an end-to-end pipeline validation orchestrator with structured JSON output. Here's what it does and what it misses.

---

### Structure

A 130-line script with:

- **`Run-Phase` helper** вҖ” wraps each phase in try/catch, times it, logs to JSON + disk
- **`Quick` mode** вҖ” skips setup and repair phases (`-Quick` flag)
- **JSON report** вҖ” writes `~/.dev-env/bootstrap-validation.json` with per-phase results
- **CI-ready** вҖ” exit 0 on all pass, exit 1 on any fail, lists failing phases
- **`Write-Log`** вҖ” consistent with the rest of the pipeline's logging pattern

Clean code. The `Run-Phase` abstraction is well done.

---

### Phase Sequence

The script runs 6 phases in this order:

```
1. 00-core-check          вҖ” prerequisites
2. 10-detect              вҖ” environment inventory
3. 60-repair -WhatIf      вҖ” dry-run repairs
4. 60-repair -Force       вҖ” actual repairs
5. 70-test                вҖ” validation checks (called "15 testЕҜ")
6. 50-setup -WhatIf       вҖ” setup dry-run preview
```

---

### Issues Found

**рҹ”ҙ Missing pipeline phases.** Compared to the canonical flow (`00 вҶ’ 30 вҶ’ 10 вҶ’ 20 вҶ’ 40 вҶ’ 50 вҶ’ 60 вҶ’ 70`), this script omits:

- **`30-clone.ps1`** вҖ” the clone that makes all other scripts available. Running this from a fresh gist deployment will fail because `scripts/` won't contain the phase scripts yet. This is the most critical gap.
- **`20-report.ps1`** вҖ” no report generated or saved
- **`40-profile.ps1`** вҖ” no profile detection, so `50-setup-home.ps1` runs blind (doesn't know if it should be home/work/lab/server)
- **`20-install-software.ps1`** вҖ” not called at all

**рҹҹЎ Wrong test count.** Line with `-Description "15 testЕҜ"` for phase 70-test. The actual script runs 17 checks. This is the 8th instance of test count drift found in the project.

**рҹҹЎ Phase ordering is non-canonical.** `60-repair` runs before `70-test` and `50-setup`. The actual pipeline runs 50 (setup) вҶ’ 60 (repair) вҶ’ 70 (test). Here it's 60 вҶ’ 70 вҶ’ 50. Running setup preview *after* repair and test is backward вҖ” you want to see what setup would do before applying repairs.

**рҹҹЎ Hardcoded profile.** Line uses `50-setup-home.ps1` unconditionally вҖ” no profile detection. On a work machine this would run the wrong setup script.

**рҹҹЎ No `-Force` handling for setup.** Quick mode skips `50-setup -WhatIf` but there's no option to run `50-setup -Force`. The script can preview setup but never apply it.

**рҹ”ө `$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"`** at the top will cause the entire script to abort on the first non-terminating error, which contradicts the phase-by-phase try/catch design. Each phase is already wrapped in try/catch, so `Stop` at the top level just means any error *outside* `Run-Phase` kills the whole thing. Minor.

**рҹ”ө Missing phases also skipped detection.** Since `40-profile.ps1` doesn't run, the `50-setup-home.ps1` call may fail on machines where `safeMode` is detected because the install script checks for `~/.dev-env/config/profile.json` and blocks if safeMode is active.

---

### What It Gets Right

- The `Run-Phase` pattern with timing and structured results is excellent
- JSON output with pass/fail/duration per phase is CI-friendly
- Exit code contract (0 = all pass, 1 = any fail) is correct
- Quick mode for fast CI feedback
- SkipBackup on repair phases (avoids backup overhead in validation runs)

---

### Fix Priority

| Priority | Issue | Fix |
|----------|-------|-----|
| рҹ”ҙ | Missing `30-clone.ps1` | Add as phase 1 вҖ” nothing else works without the repo cloned |
| рҹ”ҙ | Missing `40-profile.ps1` | Add before phase 50 so setup targets the right profile |
| рҹҹЎ | "15 testЕҜ" вҶ’ should be "17" | Update description string |
| рҹҹЎ | Phase order: 60вҶ’50вҶ’70 instead of 50вҶ’60вҶ’70 | Reorder to match canonical pipeline |
| рҹҹЎ | Hardcoded `50-setup-home.ps1` | Detect profile first, then dispatch to correct setup script |

Excellent! Now I can see the inter-script data flow clearly. Let me trace the state transfer between phases:

1. **10-detect.ps1** вҶ’ sets `$script:DetectReport` (script-scoped variable)
2. **20-report.ps1** вҶ’ reads `$script:DetectReport` via `Get-Variable -Scope Script`, OR falls back to reading from `machines.json` on disk
3. **20-report.ps1** вҶ’ sets `$script:InventoryReport` for downstream consumers
4. **60-repair.ps1** вҶ’ uses `$script:repairDedup` internally for display
5. **70-test.ps1** вҶ’ uses `$script:pass` and `$script:fail` for test tracking
6. **00-menu.ps1** вҶ’ uses `$script:categoryIndex` for menu navigation

But wait - this script-scope variable approach only works when the scripts are **dot-sourced** or called in the **same PowerShell session**. When `bootstrap.ps1` calls scripts using `& ".\scripts\10-detect.ps1"`, the scripts run in a CHILD scope (using the call operator `&`). This means:

- `& ".\scripts\10-detect.ps1"` вҶ’ runs in a new scope вҶ’ `$script:DetectReport` is set in the script's own scope
- `& ".\scripts\20-report.ps1"` вҶ’ runs in another new scope вҶ’ `$script:DetectReport` from 10-detect is NOT visible
- This means the $script:DetectReport passing mechanism **breaks** when called from bootstrap.ps1 using `&`

Unless... bootstrap.ps1 uses dot-sourcing (`. .\scripts\`) instead of `&`. Let me check how bootstrap.ps1 actually calls the scripts.

*Thinking:*

This is a major finding. The bootstrap.ps1 orchestrator is NOT a true pipeline orchestrator. It:

1. Checks git + winget (inline, not calling `00-core-check.ps1`)
2. Clones the repo (inline, not calling `30-clone.ps1`)
3. Then either:
   - **Validate-only mode:** calls `70-test.ps1` and `99-validate-bootstrap.ps1`
   - **Auto/Force mode:** calls `20-install-software.ps1` then `70-test.ps1`
   - **Interactive:** calls `00-menu.ps1` OR `20-install-software.ps1` + `70-test.ps1`

So the actual bootstrap.ps1 pipeline is:
```
Smoke test вҶ’ Clone вҶ’ Install вҶ’ Test
```

It completely SKIPS:
- `00-core-check.ps1` (does its own minimal check inline)
- `30-clone.ps1` (does its own clone inline)
- `10-detect.ps1` (NOT CALLED AT ALL)
- `20-report.ps1` (NOT CALLED AT ALL)
- `40-profile.ps1` (NOT CALLED AT ALL)
- `50-setup-*.ps1` (NOT CALLED AT ALL)
- `60-repair.ps1` (NOT CALLED AT ALL)

This means every document that says `bootstrap.ps1` runs the full pipeline `00вҶ’30вҶ’10вҶ’20вҶ’40вҶ’50вҶ’60вҶ’70` is WRONG. The actual bootstrap.ps1 is a thin orchestrator that clones, installs packages, and tests.

The full pipeline (00вҶ’30вҶ’10вҶ’20вҶ’40вҶ’50вҶ’60вҶ’70) would need to be run manually step by step, as shown in the README's manual workflow section:
```
cd ~/.dev-env/repo
./scripts/40-profile.ps1
./scripts/50-setup-home.ps1 -WhatIf
./scripts/60-repair.ps1 -WhatIf
./scripts/70-test.ps1
```

But the README, docs/index.md, architecture.md, ai/context.md, and copilot-instructions.md all claim `bootstrap.ps1` orchestrates "00вҶ’30вҶ’10вҶ’20вҶ’40вҶ’50вҶ’60вҶ’70" in one go. This is the single biggest discrepancy in the project.

Also, the `$script:DetectReport` вҶ’ `$script:InventoryReport` data flow between 10-detect and 20-report would only work if the scripts were dot-sourced into the same scope, but:
- bootstrap.ps1 uses `& ".\scripts\..."` (call operator, child scope)
- Even if they were called, they'd need to be in the same scope
- Phase scripts use `[CmdletBinding(SupportsShouldProcess=$false)]` with `param()` blocks вҖ” each script is its own scope

So even if the pipeline was complete, the `$script:DetectReport` mechanism breaks when run via `&` from an orchestrator. It would need dot-sourcing (`. .\scripts\10-detect.ps1`) for the variable to propagate.

This is a design issue: the scripts are designed to be run either standalone (each reads/writes from disk) OR chained with `$script:` variables (dot-sourced), but `bootstrap.ps1` uses `&` which creates a new scope, so neither mechanism works for inter-script data passing.

Let me also check if there's a `bootstrap.sh` issue with the `$script:DetectReport` equivalent.

## Deep Research Synthesis

### рҹ”ҙ Finding 1: `bootstrap.ps1` Does NOT Run the Documented Pipeline

This is the largest discrepancy in the project. Every document claims:

> `bootstrap.ps1` orchestrates: `00 вҶ’ 30 вҶ’ 10 вҶ’ 20 вҶ’ 40 вҶ’ 50 вҶ’ 60 вҶ’ 70`

**Actual `bootstrap.ps1` flow:**

```
Smoke test (inline) вҶ’ Clone (inline) вҶ’ Install вҶ’ Test
```

Phases actually called by `bootstrap.ps1`:

| Phase | Called? | How |
|-------|---------|-----|
| 00-core-check | **No** | Does its own inline git/winget check instead |
| 30-clone | **No** | Does its own inline clone/pull instead |
| 10-detect | **No** | Never called |
| 20-report | **No** | Never called |
| 20-install-software | **Yes** | `& ".\scripts\20-install-software.ps1"` |
| 40-profile | **No** | Never called |
| 50-setup-* | **No** | Never called |
| 60-repair | **No** | Never called |
| 70-test | **Yes** | `& ".\scripts\70-test.ps1"` |
| 99-validate | **Conditional** | Only in `-ValidateOnly` mode |

Documents affected (all claim a full pipeline that doesn't exist):
- `README.md` (lines 29, 54-68 вҖ” flow diagram, quickstart)
- `docs/index.md` (lines 51-55 вҖ” phase table)
- `docs/architecture.md` (lines 28-75 вҖ” pipeline flow)
- `ai/context.md` (lines 36-54 вҖ” architecture block)
- `copilot-instructions.md` (line 95 вҖ” phase table)
- `pipeline-flowchart.md` (entire Mermaid diagram)
- `CONTRIBUTING.md` (references to pipeline)

---

### рҹ”ҙ Finding 2: `$script:DetectReport` Inter-Scope Variable Is Broken

The design claims a `$script:` variable pass between phases:

```
10-detect.ps1  вҶ’ sets $script:DetectReport
20-report.ps1  вҶ’ reads $script:DetectReport
                 then sets $script:InventoryReport
```

**Problem:** `bootstrap.ps1` uses the call operator `& ".\scripts\10-detect.ps1"` which creates a child scope. The `$script:DetectReport` set by `10-detect.ps1` is scoped to the child script's module scope, not the parent's script scope. `20-report.ps1` then runs in a *second* child scope where `$script:DetectReport` is undefined.

Even if both scripts ran in sequence, `20-report.ps1` checks `Get-Variable -Name DetectReport -Scope Script` вҖ” but `-Scope Script` refers to `20-report.ps1`'s own scope, not the caller's scope. The flag `-Scope 1` would reach the parent.

**When it works:** Only if both scripts are dot-sourced (`. .\scripts\10-detect.ps1`) into the same scope as the caller.

**In practice:** 20-report.ps1 falls back to reading `machines.json` from disk, so data isn't lost вҖ” but the scoped variable mechanism is vestigial and doesn't function as documented.

---

### рҹ”ҙ Finding 3: `00-menu.ps1` Violates Its Own Conventions

Two direct violations of `pwsh-script-standards.instructions.md`:

**`$HOME` instead of `$env:USERPROFILE`** (line 14)
```powershell
$UserDevEnv = Join-Path $HOME ".dev-env"
# Should be: $env:USERPROFILE
```

**`$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"`** (line 11)
```powershell
$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"
# Convention says: $ErrorActionPreference = "Continue"
# This will kill the entire script on the first non-terminating error
```

---

### рҹҹЎ Finding 4: `.reasonix/` Contains Stale Run Logs

```
.reasonix/truncated-results/
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ 1780119281735-9a35da1a-web_fetch.txt
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ 1780128057314-97c160ef-run_command.txt
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ 1780184994362-482bc7b3-run_command.txt
  в””в”Җв”Җ 1780190980141-8ce7f2bd-run_command.txt
```

These are Reasonix execution artifacts (web fetch results, shell command output). They contain session timestamps and raw tool output. They're already gitignored via `.gitignore: .reasonix/` but they're consuming disk space. If this workspace was cloned, they'd exist in the repo's `.gitignore` but these are local-only.

---

### рҹҹЎ Finding 5: `index.html` (Local Landing Page) vs `docs/index.md` (Pages)

Two landing pages for different contexts:

| Dimension | `index.html` | `docs/index.md` |
|-----------|-------------|-----------------|
| Audience | Browser (local) | GitHub Pages |
| Version | v1.0.0 | v1.1.0 (stale вҖ” should be 1.1.1) |
| Content | Subset of docs | More complete |
| Scripts table | 10 entries | ~12 entries |
| AI routing | вң… Persona cards | вң… Same |
| Sync section | вқҢ Missing | вң… Present |

`index.html` at root is a standalone offline page. It's never referenced by any CI or documentation. Its version tag also lags (v1.0.0).

---

### рҹҹЎ Finding 6: Git Hooks Quality вҖ” Comprehensive but Untested

The `.github/hooks/` system is well-designed:
- **PreToolUse** (`check-ps1-format.ps1`): Checks 5 rules (shebang, aliases, path patterns, ErrorActionPreference, CmdletBinding). Blocks writes with `permissionDecision = 'ask'`.
- **PostToolUse** (`auto-format.ps1`): Tries PSScriptAnalyzer, falls back to whitespace cleanup.

However, these are CodeWhale hooks (JSON format with `PreToolUse`/`PostToolUse` events), not git hooks. They won't run in standard git operations (`git commit`, `git push`). They only run during CodeWhale tool operations. The project has no `.git/hooks/` directory for standard pre-commit linting.

---

### рҹҹЎ Finding 7: `bootstrap.sh` вҖ” 490 Lines but Missing Profile Dispatch

| Feature | `bootstrap.ps1` | `bootstrap.sh` |
|---------|-----------------|-----------------|
| Phases covered | Smoke вҶ’ Clone вҶ’ Install вҶ’ Test | 00 вҶ’ 30 вҶ’ 10 вҶ’ 20 вҶ’ 40 вҶ’ 50 |
| WhatIf/dry-run | вң… `-WhatIf` switch + `$env:DEV_ENV_WHATIF` | вң… `$DEV_ENV_WHATIF` env var only |
| Profile detection | Delegates to `40-profile.ps1` | вң… **Inline** вҖ” multi-factor detection |
| Package manager | winget | apt/brew/dnf/pacman/apk (5 managers) |
| machines.json | вң… Append with JSON array handling | вң… Same pattern via head/tail/mv |
| Broken repo handling | вң… Remove-Item + reclone | вң… git checkout HEAD -- scripts/ |
| Error handling | try/catch per phase | вқҢ `set -euo pipefail` вҖ” script-wide abort on first error |
| Logging | Transcript + Write-Log | вқҢ No logging |
| Symlink configs | вң… Conditionally | вң… Conditionally (has_repo + file exists) |
| Phase 50-70 parity | вқҢ No 50-setup, no 60-repair, no 70-test (calls powershell scripts) | вқҢ No 60-repair, no 70-test |

Key gap in `bootstrap.sh`: **No profile-aware dispatch for $PROFILE variable** вҖ” it detects a profile but never uses it to select which setup to run. All home/lab get the same packages.

---

This enables Copilot Chat to read parent-repo customizations. Minimal and correct for this workspace.

*Thinking:*

Now I have both the schema and what the scripts actually produce. Let me compare:

**Schema defines:**
- `meta` object with: bootstrap, at, repo, platform (optional? not in required?)
- `status` enum: new, same, os-changed, tools-changed
- `fingerprint`
- `hostname`, `username`, `domain`
- `os` with: caption, build, arch, kernel, installDate, lastBoot
- `tools` as additionalProperties (dynamic)
- `path` with: count, errors
- `onedrive` with: accounts, redirects
- `corporate` with: domainJoined, domain, manufacturer, model, proxy
- `changes` as string array

**10-detect.ps1 produces:**
Extra fields NOT in schema:
- `pipeline` вҖ” phases, completed, next, total
- `env` вҖ” environment info (not in schema at all)
- `meta.coreCheck` instead of `meta.bootstrap`
- `onedrive.kfm` вҖ” KFM status (not in schema)

Missing from schema:
- `pipeline` object
- `env` object
- `onedrive.kfm` field
- `meta` schema says `bootstrap` field but script uses `coreCheck`
- Schema requires `meta.repo` but script uses `$RepoUrl` (should be fine)
- Schema says `meta.platform` is optional (not in required), but it's not produced by 10-detect.ps1

**bootstrap.sh produces:**
Extra fields NOT in schema:
- `meta.wsl` вҖ” WSL flag (not in schema)

Missing from bootstrap.sh (compared to schema):
- `domain` вҖ” not produced by bootstrap.sh
- `os.build` вҖ” not produced (has caption, kernel, arch only)
- `os.installDate`, `os.lastBoot` вҖ” not produced
- `onedrive` вҖ” entirely absent (Linux has no OneDrive)
- `corporate.manufacturer`, `corporate.model`, `corporate.proxy` вҖ” only domainJoined and proxyDetected
- Schema requires `domain` in corporate but bootstrap.sh uses `proxyDetected` key which is different

The biggest issues:

1. **Schema `required` array** says `[meta, status, fingerprint, hostname, username]` but bootstrap.sh doesn't produce `domain` (it's in the schema but not in required).

2. **`meta.bootstrap` vs `meta.coreCheck`**: Schema says the version field is called `bootstrap` (and it's listed in meta.required), but 10-detect.ps1 uses `coreCheck` instead. This means Windows reports would fail schema validation since `bootstrap` is required but missing. Bootstrap.sh does use `bootstrap`.

3. **`pipeline` field**: 10-detect.ps1 adds it but it's not in the schema. Not necessarily a problem вҖ” `additionalProperties` isn't set to false, so extra fields are allowed by default.

4. **`env` field**: Same вҖ” extra but allowed.

5. **`onedrive.kfm`**: Not in schema, but allowed by default.

6. **`platform` field**: Schema expects it under `meta` as `enum: ["windows", "linux"]`. bootstrap.sh produces it. 10-detect.ps1 doesn't. Since it's not in `required`, this is fine вҖ” but it means Windows reports don't declare their platform, which is odd.

7. **`corporate.proxyDetected` vs `proxy`**: bootstrap.sh uses `proxyDetected` (boolean), schema expects `proxy` (string|null). These are semantically different вҖ” `proxyDetected` is a boolean, `proxy` is a string.

8. **Schema `$id`**: `https://doma77git.github.io/dev-env/schema/report.json` вҖ” is this URL actually reachable? Probably not without GitHub Pages being set up.

Let me present this analysis concisely.

**Assistant:**

Comparing the schema against what `10-detect.ps1` (Windows) and `bootstrap.sh` (Linux) actually produce.

---

## Schema vs Reality Analysis

### рҹ”ҙ Critical: `meta.bootstrap` vs `meta.coreCheck`

Schema declares `meta.bootstrap` as **required** (line 11: `"required": ["bootstrap", "at", "repo"]`). But:

- **`10-detect.ps1`** (line 580) produces `"coreCheck": "1.0.0"` вҖ” never sets `bootstrap`
- **`bootstrap.sh`** (line 191) correctly produces `"bootstrap": "1.1.0"`

**Result:** Every Windows report fails JSON Schema validation because the required `bootstrap` field is missing. The script uses `coreCheck` where the schema expects `bootstrap`.

---

### рҹ”ҙ `corporate.proxy` Type Mismatch

Schema defines `corporate.proxy` as `{"type": ["string", "null"]}` (line 94). But:

- **`bootstrap.sh`** (line 215) produces `"proxyDetected": $PROXY_DETECTED` вҖ” a **boolean**, not a string
- **`10-detect.ps1`** uses `$corp` which matches the schema (string or null)

**Result:** Linux reports have `proxyDetected` (boolean) instead of `proxy` (string|null). The schema key name is `proxy`, the field name differs.

---

### рҹҹЎ Windows: Missing `meta.platform`

Schema expects `meta.platform` as `enum: ["windows", "linux"]`. `bootstrap.sh` produces it. `10-detect.ps1` does **not** set `platform` in the report object (lines 579-596). Not in `required`, so validation won't fail вҖ” but it's odd to omit the platform on Windows.

---

### рҹҹЎ Windows: Extra Fields Not In Schema

`10-detect.ps1` produces two objects absent from the schema:

| Field | Line | Value |
|-------|------|-------|
| `pipeline` | 573-578 | `{ phases: {...}, completed: [...], next: "20", total: 8 }` |
| `env` | 592 | Environment info object |

Both are allowed by JSON Schema default behavior (`additionalProperties` is not restricted). They won't cause validation failures but they're undocumented contract surface.

---

### рҹҹЎ Windows: `onedrive.kfm` Not In Schema

`10-detect.ps1` (line 593) produces `onedrive.kfm` (Known Folder Move status). Schema only defines `accounts` and `redirects` under `onedrive`. Not breaking but missing from the contract.

---

### рҹҹЎ Linux: Missing Fields

`bootstrap.sh` omits several fields the schema defines:

| Schema field | Status |
|-------------|--------|
| `domain` | Not produced |
| `os.build` | Not produced |
| `os.installDate` | Not produced |
| `os.lastBoot` | Not produced |
| `onedrive` (entire object) | Not produced (correct вҖ” Linux has no OneDrive) |
| `corporate.manufacturer` | Not produced |
| `corporate.model` | Not produced |

None are in `required` so validation passes, but the data model is inconsistent between OSes.

---

### рҹҹЎ Bootstrap.sh Version Stale in Report

`bootstrap.sh` line 191 hardcodes `"bootstrap": "1.1.0"` in the generated report. The project is now v1.1.1. This means all Linux reports claim they were generated by an older bootstrap version.

---

### в„№пёҸ `$id` URL

`"$id": "https://doma77git.github.io/dev-env/schema/report.json"` вҖ” this URL resolves to the GitHub Pages site but the path `/schema/report.json` likely isn't served. Schema `$id` is a dereferenceable identifier, and this one probably returns a 404. Not a functional issue since `$schema` references the JSON Schema draft specification correctly.

---

### Summary

| # | Severity | Issue | Fix |
|---|----------|-------|-----|
| 1 | рҹ”ҙ | `meta.coreCheck` вү  `meta.bootstrap` (required field) | Change 10-detect.ps1 line 580: `coreCheck` вҶ’ `bootstrap` |
| 2 | рҹ”ҙ | `proxyDetected` (bool) вү  `proxy` (string) вҖ” key and type differ | Change bootstrap.sh line 215: `proxyDetected` вҶ’ `proxy`, use string value |
| 3 | рҹҹЎ | Windows report missing `meta.platform` | Add `platform = "windows"` to 10-detect.ps1 report |
| 4 | рҹҹЎ | Schema missing `onedrive.kfm`, `pipeline`, `env` | Add to schema OR remove from script output |
| 5 | рҹҹЎ | Linux report missing `domain`, `os.build` | Add where possible, or make schema fields optional per-platform |
| 6 | рҹҹЎ | `bootstrap.sh` hardcodes `"bootstrap": "1.1.0"` in report | Update to `1.1.1` |

---

в”Ӯ  138   51 - ## рҹ©ә Common Error Patterns
в”Ӯ  139   51 - 
в”Ӯ  140   51 - ### Error: `Unable to find type
в”Ӯ             [System.Collections.Generic.Dictionary`2]`
в”Ӯ  141   51 - **Cause:** PowerShell 5.1 instead of 7
в”Ӯ  142   51 - **Solution:**
в”Ӯ  143   51 - ```powershell
в”Ӯ  144   51 - winget install Microsoft.PowerShell
в”Ӯ  145   51 - # Nebo stГЎhni z https://github.com/PowerShell/PowerShell
в”Ӯ  146   51 - ```
в”Ӯ  147   51 - 
в”Ӯ  148   51 - ### Error: `Access to the path 'C:\Program Files...' is denied`
в”Ӯ  149   51 - **Cause:** Missing admin rights for symlink
в”Ӯ  150   51 - **Solution:**
в”Ӯ  151   51 - Enable Developer Mode in Windows Settings
в”Ӯ  152   51 - OR run as admin: `Start-Process pwsh -Verb RunAs`
в”Ӯ  153   51 - OR script falls back to `Copy-Item` (check `link-configs.ps1`)
в”Ӯ  154   51 - 
в”Ӯ  155   51 - ### Error: `git is not recognized`
в”Ӯ  156   51 - **Cause:** Git not in PATH after installation
в”Ӯ  157   51 - **Solution:**
в”Ӯ  158   51 - ```powershell
в”Ӯ  159   51 - # Refresh PATH without restarting PowerShell
в”Ӯ  160   51 - $env:Path = [Environment]::GetEnvironmentVariable("Path","Machine")
в”Ӯ             + ";" + [Environment]::GetEnvironmentVariable("Path","User")
в”Ӯ  161   51 - git --version
в”Ӯ  162   51 - ```
в”Ӯ  163   51 - 
в”Ӯ  164   51 - ### Error: `machines.json shows 'Gone: git, node'`
в”Ӯ  165   51 - **Cause:** Corrupted history from buggy version
в”Ӯ  166   51 - **Solution:**
в”Ӯ  167   51 - ```powershell
в”Ӯ  168   51 - Remove-Item ~/.dev-env/machines.json -Verbose
в”Ӯ  169   51 - ./bootstrap.ps1 # Rebuilds clean history
в”Ӯ  170   51 - ```
в”Ӯ  171   51 - 
в”Ӯ  172   51 - ### Error: `The request was aborted: Could not create SSL/TLS secure
в”Ӯ             channel`
в”Ӯ  173   51 - **Cause:** TLS 1.2 not enabled in PowerShell 5.1
в”Ӯ  174   51 - **Solution:** Already in bootstrap.ps1:
в”Ӯ  175   51 - ```powershell
в”Ӯ  176   51 - [Net.ServicePointManager]::SecurityProtocol =
в”Ӯ             [Net.SecurityProtocolType]::Tls12
в”Ӯ  177   51 - ```
в”Ӯ  178   51 - 
в”Ӯ  179   51 - ### Error: `OneDrive redirects system folders` v testech
в”Ӯ  180   51 - **Cause:** Desktop/Documents jsou v OneDrivu
в”Ӯ  181   51 - **Solution:**
в”Ӯ  182   51 - ```powershell
в”Ӯ  183   51 - .\scripts\60-repair.ps1 -Force # auto-fix (pokud KFM nenГӯ aktivnГӯ)
в”Ӯ  184   51 - # Nebo ruДҚnДӣ: OneDrive вҶ’ NastavenГӯ вҶ’ ZГЎlohovГЎnГӯ вҶ’ Spravovat
в”Ӯ             zГЎlohovГЎnГӯ
в”Ӯ  185   51 - ```
в”Ӯ  186   51 - 
в”Ӯ  187   51 - ### Error: `PATH no duplicates (Cross:15)`
в”Ӯ  188   51 - **Cause:** 15 cest je v System PATH i User PATH souДҚasnДӣ
в”Ӯ  189   51 - **Solution:**
в”Ӯ  190   51 - ```powershell

в”Ӯ  192   51 - ```

в”Ӯ  194   51 - 
в”Ӯ  195   51 - ## вң… PR/Change Validation Checklist

в”Ӯ  306   51 - 
в”Ӯ  307   51 - ## рҹ”’ HARD RULES (MUST follow вҖ” from copilot-instructions.md)
в”Ӯ  308   51 - 
в”Ӯ  309   51 - ### Safety вҖ” NEVER auto-install
в”Ӯ  310   51 - **No package manager commands without user confirmation.**
в”Ӯ  311   51 - `safeMode` profiles (work, server) block installs entirely unless
в”Ӯ             explicitly confirmed step-by-step.
в”Ӯ  312   51 - Phase `00-core-check.ps1` detects missing prerequisites вҖ” they NEVER
в”Ӯ             run `winget install`.
в”Ӯ  313   51 - Phase 30 (`30-clone.ps1`) is always read-only.
в”Ӯ  314   51 - 
в”Ӯ  315   51 - ### PowerShell scripts вҖ” header pattern
в”Ӯ  316   51 - ```powershell
в”Ӯ  317   51 - #!/usr/bin/env pwsh
в”Ӯ  318   51 - # === scripts/NAME.ps1 =========================================
в”Ӯ  319   51 - # ROLE: One-line description / ДҚeskГҪ popis
в”Ӯ  320   51 - # RUN: ./scripts/NAME.ps1 [-Switch]
в”Ӯ  321   51 - # INPUT: dependencies
в”Ӯ  322   51 - # OUTPUT: what it produces
в”Ӯ  323   51 - # ==============================================================
в”Ӯ  324   51 - ```
в”Ӯ  325   51 - 
в”Ӯ  326   51 - ### ShouldProcess contract
в”Ӯ  327   51 - All mutation scripts must:
в”Ӯ  328   51 - ```powershell
в”Ӯ  329   51 - [CmdletBinding(SupportsShouldProcess)]
в”Ӯ  330   51 - param([switch]$Force)
в”Ӯ  331   51 - ```
в”Ӯ  332   51 - 
в”Ӯ  333   51 - ### Secrets вҖ” NEVER commit
в”Ӯ  334   51 - `~/.ssh/`, `machines.json`, `~/.dev-env/config/`,
в”Ӯ             `~/.gitconfig.user`, `~/.npmrc`, `~/.aws/`, `~/.azure/`
в”Ӯ  335   51 - 
в”Ӯ ----

в”Ӯ  342   51 - 
в”Ӯ  343   51 - | Phase | Script | Purpose |

в”Ӯ             missing |

в”Ӯ             tools |

в”Ӯ             rollback) |
в”Ӯ  352   51 - | 70 | `70-test.ps1` | 16 validation checks вҶ’ exit 0=pass, 1=fail |
в”Ӯ  353   51 -

### вҡ пёҸ AGENTS.md вҖ” Regression
